# ISA tRPC API Reference

Generated by `scripts/generate-api-docs.ts`. Run:

```bash
npx tsx scripts/generate-api-docs.ts
```

## Overview

This reference documents all public tRPC procedures exported by the ISA server, including inputs, outputs, authentication requirements, and usage examples. The document is generated from the router source and runtime procedure definitions to stay in sync with the codebase.

## Router Sources

The generator scans the following files:

## Authentication

Procedures are marked as **public** (no session required) or **protected** (requires an authenticated session). Protected procedures expect a valid session cookie or equivalent authentication context when called through the API.

## Rate Limiting & Quotas

The API enforces the following rate limits (per IP):

| Limiter | Window | Max Requests | Error Code |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| apiRateLimiter | 15 minutes | 100 | RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED |
| staticRateLimiter | 15 minutes | 1000 | RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED |
| authRateLimiter | 15 minutes | 10 | AUTH_RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED |

## Error Handling

Common error codes returned by the API:

- `UNAUTHORIZED` — Authentication required or session expired.
- `FORBIDDEN` — Authenticated but lacking permissions.
- `BAD_REQUEST` — Invalid input payload.
- `NOT_FOUND` — Requested resource not found.
- `INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR` — Unhandled server error.
- `RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED` — API rate limit exceeded.
- `AUTH_RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED` — Authentication rate limit exceeded.

## Shared Types

Shared input/output shapes are defined in `shared/`. Use these modules alongside `AppRouter` to strongly type client usage.

## Procedure Details

### adminTemplates.addTemplateAction

- **Router:** `adminTemplates`
- **Procedure:** `addTemplateAction`
- **Type:** Mutation
- **Auth:** protected

#### Type Definitions

<a id="type-admintemplates-addtemplateaction"></a>
```ts
import type { AppRouter } from "../server/routers";
import type { inferRouterInputs, inferRouterOutputs } from "@trpc/server";

type AdminTemplatesAddTemplateActionInput = inferRouterInputs<AppRouter>["adminTemplates"]["addTemplateAction"];
type AdminTemplatesAddTemplateActionOutput = inferRouterOutputs<AppRouter>["adminTemplates"]["addTemplateAction"];
```

#### Example Request

```json
{
  "templateId": 0,
  "sequenceNumber": 0,
  "title": "string",
  "description": "string",
  "actionType": "string",
  "priority": "enum",
  "estimatedEffort": 0,
  "estimatedImpact": 0,
  "successCriteria": "string",
  "relatedStandards": [
    "string"
  ]
}
```

#### Example Response

```json
{
```

```json
  "sourcesCount": 0
```
```ts
};
```
